	(function(d, s, id){
	  if($('.fbCommentsPlaceholder').size()>0){
	   var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
	   if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
	   js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
	   js.src = "https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js";

<script>
  window.cfFacebookInitOptions = {
    appId            : 246441615530259,
    autoLogAppEvents : false,
    status           : true,
    xfbml            : true,
    version          : "v3.3"
  };
  window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
    FB.init(window.cfFacebookInitOptions);
  
    // Iterates over all .fb-comments elements on the page, and renders them using the FB SDK.
    // It only runs if we have not told the FB.init() to render XFBML on page load
    var renderFacebookComments = function(renderXFBMLAtLoadTime) {
      // If we have already marked XFBML to render at page load time, do not proceed.
      if(renderXFBMLAtLoadTime) { return; }
  
      var comments = document.getElementsByClassName('fb-comments');
      var i = 0;
      var len = comments.length;
      var comment = null;
      for(; i < len; i++) {
        comment = comments[i];
        FB.XFBML.parse(comment.parentElement); // comments need to be rendered/parsed from their parent element.
      }
    }
  
    renderFacebookComments(true);
  };
</script>

<script>
    
function prettyNotify(message, extra_classes, delay){
  extra_classes = (typeof(extra_classes) == 'undefined' ? '' : extra_classes);
  delay = (typeof(delay) == 'undefined' ? 3000 : delay);

  var randid = Math.random().toString(36).replace(/[^a-z]+/g, '').substr(0, 10);
  $('body').append("<div class='browserNotifier "+extra_classes+"' id='"+randid+"'>"+message+"</div>");
  $('#'+randid).velocity("slideDown", { delay: 500, duration: 2000 });
  $('#'+randid).velocity("slideUp", { delay: delay, duration: 2000 });
}

  String.prototype.hashCode = function(){
      var hash = 0;
      if (this.length == 0) return hash;
      for (i = 0; i < this.length; i++) {
          char = this.charCodeAt(i);
          hash = ((hash<<5)-hash)+char;
          hash = hash & hash; // Convert to 32bit integer
      }
      return hash;
  }

  function start_firebase(cf_uvid, funnel_id, funnel_step_id, notify_sales){
      url = 'https://cf-browser-notifier.firebaseio.com/user_pages'
      if(typeof(funnel_id) != 'undefined' && funnel_id != 'null'){
          url = url+'/'+funnel_id
      }
      if(typeof(funnel_step_id) != 'undefined' && funnel_step_id != 'null'){
          url = url+'/step_'+funnel_step_id
      } 
      if(typeof(cf_uvid) != 'undefined' && cf_uvid != 'null' && cf_uvid != ''){
          url = url+'/contacts/cf_uvid_'+cf_uvid
      } 

      var firebaseRoot = new Firebase(url);

      if(typeof(notify_sales) != 'undefined' && notify_sales != 'null'){
          firebaseRoot.child('sales').on('value', function(snapshot) {
              if(snapshot.val() != null && snapshot.val() != ''){
                  console.log(snapshot.val());
                  prettyNotify(snapshot.val());
              }
          }); 
      } 
  }

    try{
// triggering this via VWO/split testting
      //start_firebase('', 2615332, 11638438, true);
    } catch(err){
    }
 </script>

<script>
var imageData = window.CFPT.svgSwapImageData || {};

$(function () {
  $('[data-title*="svg-swap-"]').each(function () {
    var titleParts = $(this).attr('data-title').split(' ');
    var imgVarName = null;
    var animationData = null;

    $('img', this).remove();
    
    $.each(titleParts, function (index, value) {
      if (value.toLowerCase().indexOf('svg-swap-') !== -1) {
        imgVarName = value.split('-').pop();
        animationData = imageData[imgVarName];
      }
    });
    
    var params = {
        container: this,
        renderer: 'svg',
        loop: (imgVarName == 'generateLeads' || imgVarName == 'sellYourProducts') ? false : true,
        autoplay: true,
        animationData: animationData
    };

    var anim;

    //anim = bodymovin.loadAnimation(params);
    window['anim_'+imgVarName] = bodymovin.loadAnimation(params);
  });
});
</script>

  url = 'https://popping-torch-9334.firebaseio.com/appstats'

  fbRoot.child('current_users_count').on('value', function(snapshot) {
    $('[data-title="cf-counts-row"]').show();
    var target = $('[data-title="cf-users-count"] .elHeadline').first();
    var countUpOptions = {
      useEasing: true, 
      useGrouping: false, 
      separator: ',', 
      decimal: '.'
    };
    var thisCUO = countUpOptions;
    thisCUO['prefix'] = '';
    thisCUO['suffix'] = 'K';
    var current_number = target.text();
    current_number = current_number.replace(/[^0-9.]/g, "");
    var new_number = (Math.floor(snapshot.val() / 100)/10);
    var counter = new CountUp(target.get(0), current_number, new_number, 1, 2, thisCUO);
    if (!counter.error) {
      counter.start();
    } else {
      console.error(counter.error);
    }

    var total_counter = snapshot.val(); // Math.floor(snapshot.val() / 1000) * 1000;
